266: ## 8. Dependencies
267: 
268: ```
269: torch>=2.0
270: transformers>=4.30
271: segmentation-models-pytorch
272: albumentations
273: numpy
274: Pillow
275: tensorboard
276: scikit-learn
277: tqdm
278: ```
279: 
280: ---
281: 
282: ## Appendix A: RGB→Class Conversion Code
283: 
284: ```python
285: def build_color_map(labelmap_path: str) -> dict:
286:     """Parse labelmap.txt into {(r,g,b): class_id} mapping."""
287:     color_to_id = {}
288:     with open(labelmap_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
289:         for line in f:
290:             line = line.strip()
291:             if not line or line.startswith('#'):
292:                 continue
293:             parts = line.split(':')
294:             name = parts[0]
295:             rgb = tuple(map(int, parts[1].split(',')))
296:             cls_id = len(color_to_id)  # 0-indexed, in order
297:             color_to_id[rgb] = cls_id
298:     return color_to_id
299: 
300: def rgb_mask_to_class_ids(rgb_mask: np.ndarray, color_map: dict) -> np.ndarray:
301:     """Convert H×W×3 RGB mask to H×W uint8 class index mask."""
302:     class_mask = np.zeros(rgb_mask.shape[:2], dtype=np.uint8)
303:     for rgb, cls_id in color_map.items():
304:         class_mask[np.all(rgb_mask == np.array(rgb), axis=2)] = cls_id
305:     return class_mask
306: ```
307: 
308: ## Appendix B: Combo Loss Implementation
309: 
310: ```python
311: class ComboLoss(nn.Module):
312:     """α * DiceLoss + (1-α) * CrossEntropyLoss"""
313:     def __init__(self, alpha=0.5, smooth=1e-6):
314:         super().__init__()
315:         self.alpha = alpha
316:         self.smooth = smooth
317:         self.ce = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()
318: 
319:     def forward(self, pred, target):
320:         ce = self.ce(pred, target)
321:         pred_softmax = F.softmax(pred, dim=1)
322:         target_onehot = F.one_hot(target, pred.shape[1]).permute(0,3,1,2).float()
323:         intersection = (pred_softmax * target_onehot).sum(dim=(2,3))
324:         union = pred_softmax.sum(dim=(2,3)) + target_onehot.sum(dim=(2,3))
325:         dice = (2. * intersection + self.smooth) / (union + self.smooth)
326:         dice_loss = 1 - dice.mean()
327:         return self.alpha * dice_loss + (1 - self.alpha) * ce
328: ```

(End of file - total 328 lines)
</content>

The user is asking which model weights need to be downloaded. Let me give a concrete answer based on the spec and the model recommendations from the conversation.

For SegFormer-B1 via HuggingFace:
- `nvidia/segformer-b1-finetuned-ade-512-512` - this is the main pre-trained model

For the backup/alternative (U-Net via SMP):
- SMP uses ImageNet pre-trained encoders, which are downloaded automatically from torchvision/timm

Let me be concrete and list everything.

</details>

按当前方案的优先级，需要下载的权重如下：

---

## 🔽 必须下载（核心方案）

| 权重 | 模型 | 大小 | 下载方式 |
|------|------|------|---------|
| `nvidia/segformer-b1-finetuned-ade-512-512` | SegFormer-B1 本体（encoder + decoder） | ~350MB | HF 自动下载或手动 |

这是你的主力模型。首次跑 `train.py` 时 `SegformerForSemanticSegmentation.from_pretrained(...)` 会自动从 HuggingFace 拉取。也包含 ImageNet 预训练的 MiT-B1 encoder。

---

## 🔽 自动连带下载（HF 依赖）

| 权重 | 用途 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| MiT-B1 encoder | Transformers 库内置 | SegFormer-B1 加载时自动附带的 encoder backbone |
| SegformerImageProcessor config | 预处理配置 | `mean/std/size` 等，自动随模型下载 |

---

## 🔽 备用/备选权重（如果要跑 A/B 对比）

| 权重 | 模型 | 大小 | 用途 |
|------|------|------|------|
| EfficientNet-b3 (ImageNet) | U-Net backbone | ~50MB | `smp.Unet("efficientnet-b3", encoder_weights="imagenet")` 自动从 timm 下载 |
| ResNet-34 (ImageNet) | U-Net backbone | ~85MB | 同上，备选骨架 |

---

## ❌ 不需要下载的

- **SAM (ViT-B/H/L)**：不在此阶段使用，跳过
- **Mask2Former**：不在此阶段使用，跳过
- **ADE20K/Cityscapes 完整数据集**：不需要，只需要模型权重

---

## 🚀 快速预下载命令

```powershell
# 方案 1：让 Python 自动下载（HF 官方源，可能慢）
conda run -n pytorch_env python -c "from transformers import SegformerForSemanticSegmentation; SegformerForSemanticSegmentation.from_pretrained('nvidia/segformer-b1-finetuned-ade-512-512')"

# 方案 2：用国内镜像加速（推荐）
set HF_ENDPOINT=https://hf-mirror.com
conda run -n pytorch_env python -c "from transformers import SegformerForSemanticSegmentation; SegformerForSemanticSegmentation.from_pretrained('nvidia/segformer-b1-finetuned-ade-512-512')"
```

---

**总结**：就一个核心权重 `segformer-b1-finetuned-ade-512-512`（~350MB），剩下的都是自动连带下载。如果网络慢就设 `HF_ENDPOINT=https://hf-mirror.com`。

| 文件 | 用途 | 必须？ |
|------|------|--------|

| **`config.json`** (6.89 KB) | 模型结构定义（层数、类别数等） | ✅ 必须 |
| **`preprocessor_config.json`** (271 B) | 图像预处理参数（mean/std/size） | ✅ 必须 |
| `tf_model.h5` (55.1 MB) | TensorFlow 格式 —— **你用 PyTorch，不要这个** | ❌ 不需要 |
| `README.md` / `.gitattributes` | 说明文件和 git 元数据 | ❌ 不需要 |

### ⚠️ 但强烈不建议手动下载！

直接手动下 3 个文件然后拼到一起很容易路径不对、版本不匹配。正确做法是让库自动拉：

```powershell
# 一行搞定，自动拉取需要的 3 个文件
conda run -n pytorch_env python -c "from transformers import SegformerForSemanticSegmentation; SegformerForSemanticSegmentation.from_pretrained('nvidia/segformer-b1-finetuned-ade-512-512')"
```

用 `HF_ENDPOINT=https://hf-mirror.com` 加速即可。手动下载反而多花时间。

如果你已经在手动下载了，就把这 3 个文件放到同一个文件夹里，然后在代码里用本地路径加载：

```python
model = SegformerForSemanticSegmentation.from_pretrained("./segformer-b1-local/")
```

1: """
2: Plan A: SegFormer-B1 fine-tuning via HuggingFace Transformers.
3: 所有参数在 config.py 修改。直接运行: python src/train_segformer.py
4: """
5: import math
6: import random
7: from datetime import datetime
8: from pathlib import Path
9: 
10: import numpy as np
11: import torch
12: from torch.optim import AdamW
13: from torch.optim.lr_scheduler import CosineAnnealingLR, LambdaLR
14: from torch.utils.data import DataLoader
15: from torch.utils.tensorboard import SummaryWriter
16: from tqdm import tqdm
17: from transformers import SegformerForSemanticSegmentation
18: 
19: from config import (
20:     BATCH_SIZE,
21:     CLASS_NAMES,
22:     EARLY_STOP_PATIENCE,
23:     EPOCHS,
24:     EVAL_EVERY_N_EPOCHS,
25:     LEARNING_RATE,
26:     LOSS_ALPHA,
27:     NUM_CLASSES,
28:     NUM_WORKERS,
29:     PHASE1_EPOCHS,
30:     PHASE1_LR,
31:     SAVE_TOP_K,
32:     SEGFORMER_CHECKPOINT_DIR,
33:     SEGFORMER_MODEL_NAME,
34:     TRAIN_IMG_DIR,
35:     TRAIN_MASK_DIR,
36:     VAL_IMG_DIR,
37:     VAL_MASK_DIR,
38:     VIZ_EVERY_N_EPOCHS,
39:     VIZ_NUM_SAMPLES,
40:     WARMUP_STEPS,
41:     WEIGHT_DECAY,
42:     get_device,
43: )
44: from dataset import create_train_dataset, create_val_dataset
45: from losses import ComboLoss
46: 
47: 
48: # ============================================================================
49: # Metrics
50: # ============================================================================
51: 
52: 
53: def compute_iou(
54:     pred: torch.Tensor, target: torch.Tensor, num_classes: int
55: ) -> tuple[float, dict[int, float], np.ndarray]:
56:     """
57:     Compute mIoU and per-class IoU.
58: 
59:     Args:
60:         pred: (B, C, H, W) logits
61:         target: (B, H, W) class indices
62:         num_classes: number of classes
63: 
64:     Returns:
65:         miou: mean IoU across all classes
66:         per_class_iou: dict mapping class_id → IoU
67:         confusion: (num_classes, num_classes) confusion matrix
68:     """
69:     pred = pred.argmax(dim=1)  # (B, H, W)
70: 
71:     # Confusion matrix
72:     mask = (target >= 0) & (target < num_classes)
73:     pred = pred[mask]
74:     target = target[mask]
75: 
76:     # Fast confusion matrix
77:     confusion = np.zeros((num_classes, num_classes), dtype=np.int64)
78:     for t, p in zip(target.cpu().numpy().ravel(), pred.cpu().numpy().ravel()):
79:         confusion[t, p] += 1
80: 
81:     # Per-class IoU
82:     ious = {}
83:     for c in range(num_classes):
84:         intersection = confusion[c, c]
85:         union = confusion[c, :].sum() + confusion[:, c].sum() - intersection
86:         ious[c] = intersection / max(union, 1)
87: 
88:     miou = np.mean(list(ious.values()))
89:     return float(miou), ious, confusion
90: 
91: 
92: # ============================================================================
93: # Visualization
94: # ============================================================================
95: 
96: 
97: def visualize_predictions(
98:     images: torch.Tensor,
99:     masks_true: torch.Tensor,
100:     masks_pred: torch.Tensor,
101:     class_names: list[str],
102:     save_dir: Path,
103:     epoch: int,
104: ) -> None:
105:     """
106:     Save side-by-side visualization: image | ground truth | prediction.
107:     Saves as PNG with class legend.
108:     """
109:     import matplotlib
110: 
111:     matplotlib.use("Agg")
112:     import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
113:     from matplotlib.patches import Patch
114: 
115:     num_samples = min(len(images), VIZ_NUM_SAMPLES)
116:     fig, axes = plt.subplots(num_samples, 3, figsize=(15, 5 * num_samples))
117: 
118:     # Denormalize image for display
119:     mean = torch.tensor([0.485, 0.456, 0.406]).view(3, 1, 1)
120:     std = torch.tensor([0.229, 0.224, 0.225]).view(3, 1, 1)
121: 
122:     # Color map for classes
123:     from config import ID_TO_COLOR
124: 
125:     cmap = {i: (c[0] / 255, c[1] / 255, c[2] / 255) for i, c in ID_TO_COLOR.items()}
126: 
127:     for i in range(num_samples):
128:         # Denormalize
129:         img = images[i].cpu() * std + mean
130:         img = img.permute(1, 2, 0).numpy()
131:         img = np.clip(img, 0, 1)
132: 
133:         true = masks_true[i].cpu().numpy()
134:         pred_cls = masks_pred.argmax(dim=1)[i].cpu().numpy()
135: 
136:         # RGB colorization
137:         true_rgb = np.zeros((*true.shape, 3), dtype=np.float32)
138:         pred_rgb = np.zeros((*pred_cls.shape, 3), dtype=np.float32)
139: 
140:         for c, color in cmap.items():
141:             true_rgb[true == c] = color
142:             pred_rgb[pred_cls == c] = color
143: 
144:         if num_samples == 1:
145:             axes[0].imshow(img)
146:             axes[0].set_title("Original")
147:             axes[0].axis("off")
148:             axes[1].imshow(true_rgb)
149:             axes[1].set_title("Ground Truth")
150:             axes[1].axis("off")
151:             axes[2].imshow(pred_rgb)
152:             axes[2].set_title("Prediction")
153:             axes[2].axis("off")
154:         else:
155:             axes[i, 0].imshow(img)
156:             axes[i, 0].set_title("Original")
157:             axes[i, 0].axis("off")
158:             axes[i, 1].imshow(true_rgb)
159:             axes[i, 1].set_title("Ground Truth")
160:             axes[i, 1].axis("off")
161:             axes[i, 2].imshow(pred_rgb)
162:             axes[i, 2].set_title("Prediction")
163:             axes[i, 2].axis("off")
164: 
165:     # Legend
166:     legend_patches = [
167:         Patch(color=cmap[c], label=f"{c}: {name}") for c, name in enumerate(class_names)
168:     ]
169:     fig.legend(
170:         handles=legend_patches,
171:         loc="lower center",
172:         ncol=min(6, len(class_names)),
173:         fontsize=7,
174:     )
175: 
176:     plt.tight_layout(rect=[0, 0.05, 1, 1])
177:     save_path = save_dir / f"viz_epoch_{epoch:03d}.png"
178:     plt.savefig(save_path, dpi=150, bbox_inches="tight")
179:     plt.close()
180:     print(f"  Visualization saved: {save_path}")
181: 
182: 
183: # ============================================================================
184: # Training Utilities
185: # ============================================================================
186: 
187: 
188: def get_linear_warmup_cosine_scheduler(
189:     optimizer: torch.optim.Optimizer,
190:     warmup_steps: int,
191:     total_steps: int,
192:     min_lr: float = 1e-7,
193: ) -> LambdaLR:
194:     """Linear warmup → cosine decay scheduler."""
195: 
196:     def lr_lambda(step: int) -> float:
197:         if step < warmup_steps:
198:             return float(step) / max(1.0, float(warmup_steps))
199:         progress = float(step - warmup_steps) / max(1.0, float(total_steps - warmup_steps))
200:         return max(min_lr, 0.5 * (1.0 + math.cos(math.pi * progress)))
201: 
202:     return LambdaLR(optimizer, lr_lambda)
203: 
204: 
205: def save_checkpoint(
206:     model: torch.nn.Module,
207:     optimizer: torch.optim.Optimizer,
208:     epoch: int,
209:     miou: float,
210:     save_dir: Path,
211:     is_best: bool = False,
212: ) -> Path:
213:     """Save model checkpoint."""
214:     save_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
215:     fname = f"epoch_{epoch:03d}_miou_{miou:.4f}.pt" if not is_best else "best.pt"
216:     path = save_dir / fname
217:     torch.save(
218:         {
219:             "epoch": epoch,
220:             "model_state_dict": model.state_dict(),
221:             "optimizer_state_dict": optimizer.state_dict(),
222:             "miou": miou,
223:         },
224:         path,
225:     )
226:     return path
227: 
228: 
229: def cleanup_old_checkpoints(save_dir: Path, keep: int = SAVE_TOP_K) -> None:
230:     """Remove oldest checkpoints, keeping only the top N."""
231:     checkpoints = sorted(
232:         save_dir.glob("epoch_*.pt"), key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime
233:     )
234:     while len(checkpoints) > keep:
235:         oldest = checkpoints.pop(0)
236:         oldest.unlink()
237:         print(f"  Removed old checkpoint: {oldest.name}")
238: 
239: 
240: def set_encoder_grad(model: torch.nn.Module, requires_grad: bool) -> None:
241:     """Freeze or unfreeze the SegFormer encoder (MiT backbone)."""
242:     for param in model.segformer.encoder.parameters():
243:         param.requires_grad = requires_grad
244: 
245: 
246: # ============================================================================
247: # Main Training
248: # ============================================================================
249: 
250: 
251: def train() -> None:
252:     device = get_device()
253: 
254:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
255:     # Setup
256:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
257:     run_name = f"segformer_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
258:     checkpoint_dir = SEGFORMER_CHECKPOINT_DIR / run_name
259:     log_dir = Path("logs") / run_name
260:     viz_dir = checkpoint_dir / "viz"
261: 
262:     for d in [checkpoint_dir, log_dir, viz_dir]:
263:         d.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
264: 
265:     writer = SummaryWriter(log_dir=str(log_dir))
266:     print(f"Training: {run_name}")
267:     print(f"Device: {device}")
268: 
269:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
270:     # Data
271:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
272:     train_dataset = create_train_dataset(TRAIN_IMG_DIR, TRAIN_MASK_DIR)
273:     val_dataset = create_val_dataset(VAL_IMG_DIR, VAL_MASK_DIR)
274: 
275:     train_loader = DataLoader(
276:         train_dataset,
277:         batch_size=BATCH_SIZE,
278:         shuffle=True,
279:         num_workers=NUM_WORKERS,
280:         pin_memory=True,
281:         drop_last=True,
282:     )
283:     val_loader = DataLoader(
284:         val_dataset,
285:         batch_size=BATCH_SIZE,
286:         shuffle=False,
287:         num_workers=NUM_WORKERS,
288:         pin_memory=True,
289:     )
290: 
291:     print(f"Train tiles: {len(train_dataset)}, Val tiles: {len(val_dataset)}")
292:     print(
293:         f"Batches per epoch: {len(train_loader)} train, {len(val_loader)} val"
294:     )
295: 
296:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
297:     # Model
298:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
299:     print(f"Loading model: {SEGFORMER_MODEL_NAME}")
300:     model = SegformerForSemanticSegmentation.from_pretrained(
301:         SEGFORMER_MODEL_NAME,
302:         num_labels=NUM_CLASSES,
303:         ignore_mismatched_sizes=True,
304:     )
305:     model.to(device)
306: 
307:     total_params = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters())
308:     trainable_params = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters() if p.requires_grad)
309:     print(f"Parameters: {total_params:,} total, {trainable_params:,} trainable")
310: 
311:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
312:     # Loss, Optimizer, Scheduler
313:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
314:     criterion = ComboLoss(alpha=LOSS_ALPHA, num_classes=NUM_CLASSES)
315: 
316:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
317:     # Phase 1: Train decoder only (encoder frozen)
318:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
319:     print(f"\n{'='*60}")
320:     print(f"PHASE 1: Freeze encoder, train decoder ({PHASE1_EPOCHS} epochs)")
321:     print(f"{'='*60}")
322: 
323:     set_encoder_grad(model, requires_grad=False)
324:     optimizer = AdamW(
325:         filter(lambda p: p.requires_grad, model.parameters()),
326:         lr=PHASE1_LR,
327:         weight_decay=WEIGHT_DECAY,
328:     )
329: 
330:     steps_per_epoch = len(train_loader)
331:     total_steps_p1 = PHASE1_EPOCHS * steps_per_epoch
332:     scheduler = get_linear_warmup_cosine_scheduler(
333:         optimizer, warmup_steps=min(WARMUP_STEPS, total_steps_p1 // 4),
334:         total_steps=total_steps_p1
335:     )
336: 
337:     best_miou = 0.0
338:     best_epoch = 0
339:     global_step = 0
340: 
341:     for epoch in range(1, PHASE1_EPOCHS + 1):
342:         # --- Train ---
343:         model.train()
344:         train_loss = 0.0
345:         train_ce = 0.0
346:         train_dice = 0.0
347: 
348:         pbar = tqdm(train_loader, desc=f"Epoch {epoch}/{PHASE1_EPOCHS} [train]")
349:         for batch in pbar:
350:             images = batch["pixel_values"].to(device)
351:             masks = batch["labels"].to(device)
352: 
353:             outputs = model(pixel_values=images)
354:             logits = outputs.logits  # (B, C, H/4, W/4)
355: 
356:             # Upsample logits to match mask size
357:             logits = torch.nn.functional.interpolate(
358:                 logits, size=masks.shape[-2:], mode="bilinear", align_corners=False
359:             )
360: 
361:             loss, loss_dict = criterion(logits, masks)
362: 
363:             optimizer.zero_grad()
364:             loss.backward()
365:             optimizer.step()
366:             scheduler.step()
367: 
368:             train_loss += loss.item()
369:             train_ce += loss_dict["ce"]
370:             train_dice += loss_dict["dice"]
371:             global_step += 1
372: 
373:             pbar.set_postfix(
374:                 loss=f"{loss.item():.4f}",
375:                 ce=f"{loss_dict['ce']:.4f}",
376:                 dice=f"{loss_dict['dice']:.4f}",
377:                 lr=f"{scheduler.get_last_lr()[0]:.2e}",
378:             )
379: 
380:         n_batches = len(train_loader)
381:         avg_loss = train_loss / n_batches
382:         writer.add_scalar("train/loss", avg_loss, epoch)
383:         writer.add_scalar("train/ce_loss", train_ce / n_batches, epoch)
384:         writer.add_scalar("train/dice_loss", train_dice / n_batches, epoch)
385:         writer.add_scalar("lr", scheduler.get_last_lr()[0], epoch)
386: 
387:         # --- Validate ---
388:         if epoch % EVAL_EVERY_N_EPOCHS == 0 or epoch == PHASE1_EPOCHS:
389:             miou = validate(model, val_loader, criterion, writer, epoch)
390:             print(f"  Val mIoU: {miou:.4f}")
391: 
392:             if miou > best_miou:
393:                 best_miou = miou
394:                 best_epoch = epoch
395:                 save_checkpoint(model, optimizer, epoch, miou, checkpoint_dir, is_best=True)
396:                 print(f"  New best mIoU: {best_miou:.4f} ✓")
397: 
398:             save_checkpoint(model, optimizer, epoch, miou, checkpoint_dir)
399:             cleanup_old_checkpoints(checkpoint_dir)
400: 
401:             if epoch % VIZ_EVERY_N_EPOCHS == 0:
402:                 _viz_val_samples(model, val_dataset, viz_dir, epoch)
403: 
404:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
405:     # Phase 2: Unfreeze all, fine-tune
406:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
407:     remaining_epochs = EPOCHS - PHASE1_EPOCHS
408:     print(f"\n{'='*60}")
409:     print(f"PHASE 2: Unfreeze all, fine-tune ({remaining_epochs} epochs)")
410:     print(f"{'='*60}")
411: 
412:     set_encoder_grad(model, requires_grad=True)
413:     optimizer = AdamW(model.parameters(), lr=LEARNING_RATE, weight_decay=WEIGHT_DECAY)
414:     total_steps_p2 = remaining_epochs * steps_per_epoch
415:     scheduler = get_linear_warmup_cosine_scheduler(
416:         optimizer,
417:         warmup_steps=min(WARMUP_STEPS, total_steps_p2 // 4),
418:         total_steps=total_steps_p2,
419:     )
420: 
421:     patience_counter = 0
422: 
423:     for epoch in range(PHASE1_EPOCHS + 1, EPOCHS + 1):
424:         # --- Train ---
425:         model.train()
426:         train_loss = 0.0
427:         train_ce = 0.0
428:         train_dice = 0.0
429: 
430:         pbar = tqdm(train_loader, desc=f"Epoch {epoch}/{EPOCHS} [train]")
431:         for batch in pbar:
432:             images = batch["pixel_values"].to(device)
433:             masks = batch["labels"].to(device)
434: 
435:             outputs = model(pixel_values=images)
436:             logits = outputs.logits
437:             logits = torch.nn.functional.interpolate(
438:                 logits, size=masks.shape[-2:], mode="bilinear", align_corners=False
439:             )
440: 
441:             loss, loss_dict = criterion(logits, masks)
442: 
443:             optimizer.zero_grad()
444:             loss.backward()
445:             optimizer.step()
446:             scheduler.step()
447: 
448:             train_loss += loss.item()
449:             train_ce += loss_dict["ce"]
450:             train_dice += loss_dict["dice"]
451: 
452:             pbar.set_postfix(
453:                 loss=f"{loss.item():.4f}",
454:                 ce=f"{loss_dict['ce']:.4f}",
455:                 dice=f"{loss_dict['dice']:.4f}",
456:                 lr=f"{scheduler.get_last_lr()[0]:.2e}",
457:             )
458: 
459:         avg_loss = train_loss / n_batches
460:         writer.add_scalar("train/loss", avg_loss, epoch)
461:         writer.add_scalar("train/ce_loss", train_ce / n_batches, epoch)
462:         writer.add_scalar("train/dice_loss", train_dice / n_batches, epoch)
463:         writer.add_scalar("lr", scheduler.get_last_lr()[0], epoch)
464: 
465:         # --- Validate ---
466:         if epoch % EVAL_EVERY_N_EPOCHS == 0 or epoch == EPOCHS:
467:             miou = validate(model, val_loader, criterion, writer, epoch)
468:             print(f"  Val mIoU: {miou:.4f} (best: {best_miou:.4f} @ epoch {best_epoch})")
469: 
470:             if miou > best_miou:
471:                 best_miou = miou
472:                 best_epoch = epoch
473:                 patience_counter = 0
474:                 save_checkpoint(model, optimizer, epoch, miou, checkpoint_dir, is_best=True)
475:                 print(f"  New best mIoU: {best_miou:.4f} ✓")
476:             else:
477:                 patience_counter += 1
478: 
479:             save_checkpoint(model, optimizer, epoch, miou, checkpoint_dir)
480:             cleanup_old_checkpoints(checkpoint_dir)
481: 
482:             if epoch % VIZ_EVERY_N_EPOCHS == 0:
483:                 _viz_val_samples(model, val_dataset, viz_dir, epoch)
484: 
485:         # Early stopping
486:         if patience_counter >= EARLY_STOP_PATIENCE:
487:             print(f"\nEarly stopping at epoch {epoch} (no improvement for {EARLY_STOP_PATIENCE} evals)")
488:             break
489: 
490:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
491:     # Done
492:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
493:     print(f"\n{'='*60}")
494:     print(f"Training complete!")
495:     print(f"Best mIoU: {best_miou:.4f} at epoch {best_epoch}")
496:     print(f"Checkpoint: {checkpoint_dir / 'best.pt'}")
497:     writer.close()
498: 
499: 
500: # ============================================================================
501: # Validation
502: # ============================================================================
503: 
504: 
505: @torch.no_grad()
506: def validate(
507:     model: torch.nn.Module,
508:     val_loader: DataLoader,
509:     criterion: ComboLoss,
510:     writer: SummaryWriter,
511:     epoch: int,
512: ) -> float:
513:     """Run validation and log metrics."""
514:     model.eval()
515:     val_loss = 0.0
516:     all_preds = []
517:     all_targets = []
518: 
519:     for batch in tqdm(val_loader, desc="  Validating", leave=False):
520:         images = batch["pixel_values"].to(device)
521:         masks = batch["labels"].to(device)
522: 
523:         outputs = model(pixel_values=images)
524:         logits = outputs.logits
525:         logits = torch.nn.functional.interpolate(
526:             logits, size=masks.shape[-2:], mode="bilinear", align_corners=False
527:         )
528: 
529:         loss, _ = criterion(logits, masks)
530:         val_loss += loss.item()
531: 
532:         all_preds.append(logits.cpu())
533:         all_targets.append(masks.cpu())
534: 
535:     avg_loss = val_loss / len(val_loader)
536:     writer.add_scalar("val/loss", avg_loss, epoch)
537: 
538:     # Compute mIoU
539:     all_preds = torch.cat(all_preds, dim=0)
540:     all_targets = torch.cat(all_targets, dim=0)
541:     miou, per_class_iou, _ = compute_iou(all_preds, all_targets, NUM_CLASSES)
542: 
543:     writer.add_scalar("val/mIoU", miou, epoch)
544: 
545:     # Log per-class IoU
546:     for cls_id, iou in per_class_iou.items():
547:         writer.add_scalar(f"val/IoU_{CLASS_NAMES[cls_id]}", iou, epoch)
548: 
549:     # Print per-class summary
550:     iou_str = " | ".join(
551:         f"{name}: {iou:.3f}"
552:         for name, (cls_id, iou) in zip(CLASS_NAMES, per_class_iou.items())
553:     )
554:     print(f"  Per-class IoU: {iou_str}")
555: 
556:     return miou
557: 
558: 
559: def _viz_val_samples(
560:     model: torch.nn.Module,
561:     val_dataset,
562:     viz_dir: Path,
563:     epoch: int,
564: ) -> None:
565:     """Generate visualization from a few validation samples."""
566:     model.eval()
567:     indices = random.sample(range(len(val_dataset)), min(VIZ_NUM_SAMPLES, len(val_dataset)))
568: 
569:     images_list = []
570:     masks_true_list = []
571:     masks_pred_list = []
572: 
573:     for idx in indices:
574:         sample = val_dataset[idx]
575:         image = sample["pixel_values"].unsqueeze(0).to(device)
576:         mask_true = sample["labels"].unsqueeze(0).to(device)
577: 
578:         with torch.no_grad():
579:             outputs = model(pixel_values=image)
580:             logits = outputs.logits
581:             logits = torch.nn.functional.interpolate(
582:                 logits, size=mask_true.shape[-2:], mode="bilinear", align_corners=False
583:             )
584: 
585:         images_list.append(image.squeeze(0).cpu())
586:         masks_true_list.append(mask_true.squeeze(0).cpu())
587:         masks_pred_list.append(logits.squeeze(0).cpu())
588: 
589:     images_batch = torch.stack(images_list)
590:     masks_true_batch = torch.stack(masks_true_list)
591:     masks_pred_batch = torch.stack(masks_pred_list)
592: 
593:     visualize_predictions(
594:         images_batch, masks_true_batch, masks_pred_batch,
595:         CLASS_NAMES, viz_dir, epoch,
596:     )
597: 
598: 
599: # ============================================================================
600: # Entry
601: # ============================================================================
602: 
603: if __name__ == "__main__":
604:     train()

(End of file - total 604 lines)
</content>
```

133: # 手工指定示例: EVAL_CHECKPOINT = CHECKPOINT_DIR / "segformer" / "20260522_143000" / "best.pt"
134: EVAL_CHECKPOINT = None  # None = 自动扫描
135: 
136: 
137: def auto_find_checkpoint(model_type: str) -> Path | None:
138:     """自动找到模型目录下最新的 best.pt."""
139:     base = CHECKPOINT_DIR / model_type
140:     if not base.exists():
141:         return None
142:     runs = [d for d in base.iterdir() if d.is_dir()]
143:     bests = []
144:     for run in runs:
145:         pt = run / "best.pt"
146:         if pt.exists():
147:             bests.append((pt.stat().st_mtime, pt))
148:     if not bests:
149:         return None
150:     bests.sort(reverse=True)
151:     return bests[0][1]

<path>E:\CVAT\src\dataset.py</path>

<content>
1: """
2: PyTorch Dataset for semantic segmentation tiles.
3: Supports on-the-fly Albumentations augmentation (train) and clean loading (val).
4: """
5: from pathlib import Path
6: from typing import Optional
7: 
8: import albumentations as A
9: import numpy as np
10: import torch
11: from PIL import Image
12: from torch.utils.data import Dataset
13: 
14: from config import IMAGE_SIZE
15: 
16: 
17: # ============================================================================
18: # Augmentation pipelines
19: # ============================================================================
20: 
21: IMAGENET_MEAN = (0.485, 0.456, 0.406)
22: IMAGENET_STD = (0.229, 0.224, 0.225)
23: 
24: 
25: def get_train_transforms(image_size: int = IMAGE_SIZE) -> A.Compose:
26:     """
27:     Aggressive augmentation for small-dataset training.
28: 
29:     Spatial transforms (applied to image+mask):
30:       - RandomResizedCrop: scale 0.5-1.0 → effective 5-10× dataset expansion
31:       - HorizontalFlip: scene symmetry
32:       - Rotate(±30°): orientation invariance
33:       - ElasticTransform: deformation robustness
34: 
35:     Pixel transforms (image only):
36:       - BrightnessContrast: lighting variation
37:       - HueSaturationValue: color variation
38:       - GaussNoise: sensor noise robustness
39: 
40:     Normalization: ImageNet mean/std (SegFormer & EfficientNet both use it).
41:     """
42:     return A.Compose(
43:         [
44:             A.RandomResizedCrop(
45:                 size=(image_size, image_size),
46:                 scale=(0.5, 1.0),
47:                 ratio=(0.9, 1.1),
48:                 p=1.0,
49:             ),
50:             A.HorizontalFlip(p=0.5),
51:             A.Rotate(limit=30, border_mode=0, p=0.7),
52:             A.ElasticTransform(alpha=1, sigma=50, alpha_affine=50, p=0.3),
53:             A.BrightnessContrast(brightness_limit=0.2, contrast_limit=0.2, p=0.7),
54:             A.HueSaturationValue(
55:                 hue_shift_limit=15, sat_shift_limit=20, val_shift_limit=20, p=0.4
56:             ),
57:             A.GaussNoise(var_limit=(10.0, 50.0), p=0.3),
58:             A.Normalize(
59:                 mean=IMAGENET_MEAN, std=IMAGENET_STD, max_pixel_value=255.0
60:             ),
61:         ]
62:     )
63: 
64: 
65: def get_val_transforms() -> A.Compose:
66:     """Validation: no augmentation, only ImageNet normalization."""
67:     return A.Compose(
68:         [
69:             A.Normalize(
70:                 mean=IMAGENET_MEAN, std=IMAGENET_STD, max_pixel_value=255.0
71:             ),
72:         ]
73:     )
74: 
75: 
76: # ============================================================================
77: # Dataset
78: # ============================================================================
79: 
80: 
81: class SegmentationDataset(Dataset):
82:     """
83:     Loads tile images and masks from preprocessed data/ directory.
84: 
85:     Args:
86:         img_dir: Directory containing tile images (*.png).
87:         mask_dir: Directory containing tile masks (*.png, single-channel).
88:         transforms: Albumentations Compose (None = raw loading).
89:     """
90: 
91:     def __init__(
92:         self,
93:         img_dir: Path,
94:         mask_dir: Path,
95:         transforms: Optional[A.Compose] = None,
96:     ):
97:         self.img_dir = Path(img_dir)
98:         self.mask_dir = Path(mask_dir)
99:         self.transforms = transforms
100: 
101:         self.file_names = sorted(
102:             [p.name for p in self.img_dir.glob("*.png")]
103:         )
104: 
105:         if not self.file_names:
106:             raise RuntimeError(f"No PNG files found in {self.img_dir}")
107: 
108:         # Verify masks exist
109:         missing_masks = [
110:             f for f in self.file_names if not (self.mask_dir / f).exists()
111:         ]
112:         if missing_masks:
113:             raise RuntimeError(
114:                 f"Missing masks for {len(missing_masks)} tiles: {missing_masks[:5]}..."
115:             )
116: 
117:     def __len__(self) -> int:
118:         return len(self.file_names)
119: 
120:     def __getitem__(self, idx: int) -> dict[str, torch.Tensor]:
121:         fname = self.file_names[idx]
122: 
123:         # Load image (H, W, 3) RGB
124:         image = np.array(Image.open(self.img_dir / fname).convert("RGB"))
125: 
126:         # Load mask (H, W) single-channel, convert to int64 class indices
127:         mask = np.array(Image.open(self.mask_dir / fname), dtype=np.int64)
128: 
129:         # Apply transforms (Albumentations expects contiguous uint8 arrays)
130:         # A.Normalize outputs float32 in [0,1] with mean/std applied
131:         if self.transforms is not None:
132:             augmented = self.transforms(image=np.ascontiguousarray(image), mask=mask)
133:             image = augmented["image"]  # float32 (H, W, 3), normalized
134:             mask = augmented["mask"]     # uint8 (H, W)
135:             # Channel-first for PyTorch
136:             image = torch.from_numpy(image).permute(2, 0, 1)
137:         else:
138:             # Fallback: no transforms, do manual [0,1] scaling
139:             image = torch.from_numpy(image).permute(2, 0, 1).float() / 255.0
140: 
141:         mask = torch.from_numpy(mask).long()
142: 
143:         return {"pixel_values": image, "labels": mask}
144: 
145: 
146: # ============================================================================
147: # Factory functions
148: # ============================================================================
149: 
150: 
151: def create_train_dataset(
152:     img_dir: Path, mask_dir: Path
153: ) -> SegmentationDataset:
154:     """Create training dataset with full augmentation."""
155:     return SegmentationDataset(
156:         img_dir=img_dir,
157:         mask_dir=mask_dir,
158:         transforms=get_train_transforms(),
159:     )
160: 
161: 
162: def create_val_dataset(
163:     img_dir: Path, mask_dir: Path
164: ) -> SegmentationDataset:
165:     """Create validation dataset without augmentation."""
166:     return SegmentationDataset(
167:         img_dir=img_dir,
168:         mask_dir=mask_dir,
169:         transforms=get_val_transforms(),
170:     )

(End of file - total 170 lines)
</content>

<content>
1: """
2: Preprocessing: RGB mask → class index, tiling, train/val split.
3: 
4: Run once before training:
5:     python src/preprocess.py
6: 
7: Input:  南原图/*.JPG + 南新/SegmentationClass/*.png
8: Output: data/{train,val}/{images,masks}/*.png (512×512 tiles)
9: """
10: from __future__ import annotations
11: 
12: import random
13: from pathlib import Path
14: 
15: import numpy as np
16: from PIL import Image
17: from tqdm import tqdm
18: 
19: from config import (
20:     COLOR_TO_ID,
21:     IMAGE_SIZE,
22:     IMAGESET_PATH,
23:     ORIGINAL_IMG_DIR,
24:     RANDOM_SEED,
25:     SEGCLASS_DIR,
26:     TILE_STRIDE,
27:     TRAIN_IMG_DIR,
28:     TRAIN_MASK_DIR,
29:     TRAIN_SPLIT,
30:     VAL_IMG_DIR,
31:     VAL_MASK_DIR,
32: )
33: 
34: 
35: def parse_imageset(imageset_path: Path) -> list[str]:
36:     """Parse ImageSets file, return list of base names (without extension)."""
37:     names = []
38:     with open(imageset_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
39:         for line in f:
40:             name = line.strip()
41:             if name:
42:                 names.append(name)
43:     return names
44: 
45: 
46: def find_image_path(base_name: str) -> Path | None:
47:     """Find the actual image file given base name. Try .JPG then .jpg."""
48:     for ext in (".JPG", ".jpg"):
49:         p = ORIGINAL_IMG_DIR / f"{base_name}{ext}"
50:         if p.exists():
51:             return p
52:     return None
53: 
54: 
55: def find_mask_path(base_name: str) -> Path | None:
56:     """Find the corresponding SegmentationClass mask file."""
57:     p = SEGCLASS_DIR / f"{base_name}.png"
58:     return p if p.exists() else None
59: 
60: 
61: def rgb_mask_to_class_ids(
62:     rgb_mask: np.ndarray, color_to_id: dict[tuple[int, ...], int]
63: ) -> np.ndarray:
64:     """
65:     Convert H×W×3 RGB mask to H×W uint8 class index mask.
66: 
67:     Args:
68:         rgb_mask: (H, W, 3) numpy array, dtype=uint8
69:         color_to_id: mapping from (r,g,b) tuple to class index
70: 
71:     Returns:
72:         (H, W) numpy array, dtype=uint8
73:     """
74:     class_mask = np.zeros(rgb_mask.shape[:2], dtype=np.uint8)
75:     for rgb, cls_id in color_to_id.items():
76:         class_mask[np.all(rgb_mask == np.array(rgb), axis=2)] = cls_id
77:     return class_mask
78: 
79: 
80: def tile_positions(h: int, w: int, size: int, stride: int) -> list[tuple[int, int]]:
81:     """
82:     Compute (y, x) top-left positions for overlapping tiles.
83: 
84:     Covers the entire image including right/bottom edges.
85:     """
86:     y_positions = list(range(0, h - size + 1, stride))
87:     x_positions = list(range(0, w - size + 1, stride))
88: 
89:     # Edge fill: add last valid position at bottom/right edge
90:     if h > size and (h - size) not in y_positions:
91:         y_positions.append(h - size)
92:     if w > size and (w - size) not in x_positions:
93:         x_positions.append(w - size)
94: 
95:     # If image smaller than tile size, just one tile from (0,0)
96:     if not y_positions:
97:         y_positions = [0]
98:     if not x_positions:
99:         x_positions = [0]
100: 
101:     y_positions = sorted(set(y_positions))
102:     x_positions = sorted(set(x_positions))
103: 
104:     return [(y, x) for y in y_positions for x in x_positions]
105: 
106: 
107: def save_tile(img: np.ndarray, out_path: Path) -> None:
108:     """Save a tile as PNG."""
109:     Image.fromarray(img).save(out_path)
110: 
111: 
112: def main() -> None:
113:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
114:     # 1. Discover valid image-mask pairs
115:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
116:     all_names = parse_imageset(IMAGESET_PATH)
117:     print(f"[1/4] ImageSet entries: {len(all_names)}")
118: 
119:     valid_pairs: list[tuple[str, Path, Path]] = []
120:     missing: list[str] = []
121: 
122:     for name in all_names:
123:         img_path = find_image_path(name)
124:         mask_path = find_mask_path(name)
125:         if img_path and mask_path:
126:             valid_pairs.append((name, img_path, mask_path))
127:         else:
128:             missing.append(name)
129: 
130:     if missing:
131:         print(f"  WARNING: {len(missing)} images missing — skipped: {missing}")
132:     print(f"  Valid image-mask pairs: {len(valid_pairs)}")
133: 
134:     if not valid_pairs:
135:         print("ERROR: No valid image-mask pairs found. Aborting.")
136:         return
137: 
138:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
139:     # 2. Train/val split at original image level
140:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
141:     random.seed(RANDOM_SEED)
142:     random.shuffle(valid_pairs)
143:     split_idx = int(len(valid_pairs) * TRAIN_SPLIT)
144: 
145:     train_pairs = valid_pairs[:split_idx]
146:     val_pairs = valid_pairs[split_idx:]
147:     print(f"[2/4] Split: {len(train_pairs)} train / {len(val_pairs)} val")
148: 
149:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
150:     # 3. Process: RGB→class index → tile → save
151:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
152:     for d in [TRAIN_IMG_DIR, TRAIN_MASK_DIR, VAL_IMG_DIR, VAL_MASK_DIR]:
153:         d.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
154: 
155:     color_to_id = COLOR_TO_ID
156:     total_train = 0
157:     total_val = 0
158: 
159:     print("[3/4] Processing tiles...")
160: 
161:     for split_name, pairs, img_dir, mask_dir in [
162:         ("train", train_pairs, TRAIN_IMG_DIR, TRAIN_MASK_DIR),
163:         ("val", val_pairs, VAL_IMG_DIR, VAL_MASK_DIR),
164:     ]:
165:         for name, img_path, mask_path in tqdm(
166:             pairs, desc=f"  {split_name}"
167:         ):
168:             # Load
169:             image = np.array(Image.open(img_path).convert("RGB"))
170:             mask_rgb = np.array(Image.open(mask_path).convert("RGB"))
171: 
172:             if image.shape[:2] != mask_rgb.shape[:2]:
173:                 print(
174:                     f"  WARNING: shape mismatch for {name} "
175:                     f"(image {image.shape[:2]} vs mask {mask_rgb.shape[:2]}), skipping"
176:                 )
177:                 continue
178: 
179:             # Convert RGB mask to class indices
180:             mask_idx = rgb_mask_to_class_ids(mask_rgb, color_to_id)
181: 
182:             # Tile
183:             positions = tile_positions(
184:                 image.shape[0], image.shape[1], IMAGE_SIZE, TILE_STRIDE
185:             )
186: 
187:             for y, x in positions:
188:                 tile_img = image[y : y + IMAGE_SIZE, x : x + IMAGE_SIZE]
189:                 tile_mask = mask_idx[y : y + IMAGE_SIZE, x : x + IMAGE_SIZE]
190: 
191:                 tile_name = f"{name}_y{y}_x{x}.png"
192:                 save_tile(tile_img, img_dir / tile_name)
193:                 # mode="L" for single-channel grayscale
194:                 Image.fromarray(tile_mask, mode="L").save(mask_dir / tile_name)
195: 
196:                 if split_name == "train":
197:                     total_train += 1
198:                 else:
199:                     total_val += 1
200: 
201:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
202:     # 4. Summary
203:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
204:     print(f"[4/4] Done!")
205:     print(f"  Train tiles: {total_train} ({len(train_pairs)} source images)")
206:     print(f"  Val tiles:   {total_val} ({len(val_pairs)} source images)")
207:     print(f"  Total:       {total_train + total_val}")
208:     print(f"\n  Output dirs:")
209:     print(f"    {TRAIN_IMG_DIR}")
210:     print(f"    {TRAIN_MASK_DIR}")
211:     print(f"    {VAL_IMG_DIR}")
212:     print(f"    {VAL_MASK_DIR}")
213: 
214: 
215: if __name__ == "__main__":
216:     main()

(End of file - total 216 lines)
</content>

<path>E:\CVAT\src\losses.py</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: """
2: Loss functions for semantic segmentation.
3: ComboLoss = α * DiceLoss + (1-α) * CrossEntropyLoss
4: """
5: import torch
6: import torch.nn as nn
7: import torch.nn.functional as F
8: 
9: 
10: class ComboLoss(nn.Module):
11:     """
12:     α * DiceLoss + (1-α) * CrossEntropyLoss
13: 
14:     Dice handles class imbalance naturally (intersection-over-union based).
15:     CE provides smooth, stable gradients.
16: 
17:     Args:
18:         alpha: Weight for Dice loss (0-1). Default 0.5 gives equal weight.
19:         smooth: Smoothing factor for Dice to avoid division by zero.
20:         num_classes: Number of classes for one-hot encoding.
21:     """
22: 
23:     def __init__(self, alpha: float = 0.5, smooth: float = 1e-6, num_classes: int = 11):
24:         super().__init__()
25:         self.alpha = alpha
26:         self.smooth = smooth
27:         self.num_classes = num_classes
28:         self.ce = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()
29: 
30:     def forward(
31:         self, pred: torch.Tensor, target: torch.Tensor
32:     ) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, dict[str, float]]:
33:         """
34:         Args:
35:             pred: (B, C, H, W) raw logits
36:             target: (B, H, W) class indices (int64)
37: 
38:         Returns:
39:             total_loss: scalar loss
40:             loss_dict: {"ce": float, "dice": float} for logging
41:         """
42:         ce_loss = self.ce(pred, target)
43: 
44:         # Dice loss: compute per class, then average
45:         pred_softmax = F.softmax(pred, dim=1)  # (B, C, H, W)
46:         target_onehot = (
47:             F.one_hot(target, num_classes=self.num_classes)
48:             .permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
49:             .float()
50:         )  # (B, C, H, W)
51: 
52:         intersection = (pred_softmax * target_onehot).sum(dim=(0, 2, 3))  # (C,)
53:         cardinality = pred_softmax.sum(dim=(0, 2, 3)) + target_onehot.sum(
54:             dim=(0, 2, 3)
55:         )  # (C,)
56: 
57:         dice_score = (2.0 * intersection + self.smooth) / (cardinality + self.smooth)  # (C,)
58:         dice_loss = 1.0 - dice_score.mean()
59: 
60:         total_loss = self.alpha * dice_loss + (1.0 - self.alpha) * ce_loss
61: 
62:         return total_loss, {"ce": ce_loss.item(), "dice": dice_loss.item()}
63: 
64: 
65: class DiceLoss(nn.Module):
66:     """Pure Dice loss for reference / experimentation."""
67: 
68:     def __init__(self, smooth: float = 1e-6, num_classes: int = 11):
69:         super().__init__()
70:         self.smooth = smooth
71:         self.num_classes = num_classes
72: 
73:     def forward(self, pred: torch.Tensor, target: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
74:         pred_softmax = F.softmax(pred, dim=1)
75:         target_onehot = (
76:             F.one_hot(target, num_classes=self.num_classes)
77:             .permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
78:             .float()
79:         )
80:         intersection = (pred_softmax * target_onehot).sum(dim=(0, 2, 3))
81:         cardinality = pred_softmax.sum(dim=(0, 2, 3)) + target_onehot.sum(
82:             dim=(0, 2, 3)
83:         )
84:         dice_score = (2.0 * intersection + self.smooth) / (cardinality + self.smooth)
85:         return 1.0 - dice_score.mean()

(End of file - total 85 lines)
</content>

<content>
1: """
2: Shared evaluation script for both Plan A (SegFormer) and Plan B (U-Net).
3: 在 config.py 修改 EVAL_MODEL_TYPE 和 EVAL_CHECKPOINT。
4: 直接运行: python src/evaluate.py
5: """
6: import json
7: from pathlib import Path
8: 
9: import numpy as np
10: import torch
11: from torch.utils.data import DataLoader
12: from tqdm import tqdm
13: 
14: from config import (
15:     BATCH_SIZE,
16:     CLASS_NAMES,
17:     EVAL_CHECKPOINT,
18:     EVAL_MODEL_TYPE,
19:     NUM_CLASSES,
20:     NUM_WORKERS,
21:     SEGFORMER_MODEL_NAME,
22:     UNET_ENCODER,
23:     UNET_ENCODER_WEIGHTS,
24:     VAL_IMG_DIR,
25:     VAL_MASK_DIR,
26:     VIZ_NUM_SAMPLES,
27:     ID_TO_COLOR,
28:     auto_find_checkpoint,
29:     get_device,
30: )
31: from dataset import create_val_dataset
32: 
33: 
34: # ============================================================================
35: # Metrics
36: # ============================================================================
37: 
38: 
39: def compute_metrics(
40:     pred: torch.Tensor, target: torch.Tensor, num_classes: int
41: ) -> dict:
42:     """
43:     Compute comprehensive metrics: mIoU, per-class IoU, pixel accuracy, Dice.
44: 
45:     Args:
46:         pred: (B, C, H, W) logits
47:         target: (B, H, W) class indices
48:         num_classes: number of classes
49: 
50:     Returns:
51:         dict with miou, per_class_iou, pixel_accuracy, per_class_dice, confusion_matrix
52:     """
53:     pred_cls = pred.argmax(dim=1).cpu().numpy()
54:     target = target.cpu().numpy()
55: 
56:     mask = (target >= 0) & (target < num_classes)
57: 
58:     # Confusion matrix
59:     confusion = np.zeros((num_classes, num_classes), dtype=np.int64)
60:     for t, p in zip(target[mask].ravel(), pred_cls[mask].ravel()):
61:         confusion[t, p] += 1
62: 
63:     # Per-class IoU
64:     ious = {}
65:     dices = {}
66:     for c in range(num_classes):
67:         intersection = confusion[c, c]
68:         union = confusion[c, :].sum() + confusion[:, c].sum() - intersection
69:         ious[c] = float(intersection / max(union, 1))
70: 
71:         # Dice = 2*TP / (2*TP + FP + FN)
72:         dice_denom = confusion[c, :].sum() + confusion[:, c].sum()
73:         dices[c] = float(2 * intersection / max(dice_denom, 1))
74: 
75:     # Pixel accuracy
76:     correct = confusion.diagonal().sum()
77:     total = confusion.sum()
78:     pixel_acc = float(correct / max(total, 1))
79: 
80:     # Mean metrics
81:     miou = float(np.mean(list(ious.values())))
82:     mdice = float(np.mean(list(dices.values())))
83: 
84:     return {
85:         "miou": miou,
86:         "mdice": mdice,
87:         "pixel_accuracy": pixel_acc,
88:         "per_class_iou": ious,
89:         "per_class_dice": dices,
90:         "confusion_matrix": confusion.tolist(),
91:     }
92: 
93: 
94: # ============================================================================
95: # Visualization
96: # ============================================================================
97: 
98: 
99: def generate_visualizations(
100:     model: torch.nn.Module,
101:     val_dataset,
102:     model_type: str,
103:     output_dir: Path,
104:     device: str,
105:     num_samples: int = VIZ_NUM_SAMPLES,
106: ) -> None:
107:     """Generate and save prediction visualizations."""
108:     import matplotlib
109: 
110:     matplotlib.use("Agg")
111:     import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
112:     from matplotlib.patches import Patch
113: 
114:     model.eval()
115: 
116:     import random
117:     random.seed(42)
118:     indices = random.sample(
119:         range(len(val_dataset)), min(num_samples, len(val_dataset))
120:     )
121: 
122:     mean = torch.tensor([0.485, 0.456, 0.406]).view(3, 1, 1)
123:     std = torch.tensor([0.229, 0.224, 0.225]).view(3, 1, 1)
124:     cmap = {i: (c[0] / 255, c[1] / 255, c[2] / 255) for i, c in ID_TO_COLOR.items()}
125: 
126:     fig, axes = plt.subplots(len(indices), 3, figsize=(15, 5 * len(indices)))
127:     if len(indices) == 1:
128:         axes = np.array([axes])
129: 
130:     for row, idx in enumerate(indices):
131:         sample = val_dataset[idx]
132:         image_t = sample["pixel_values"].unsqueeze(0).to(device)
133:         mask_true = sample["labels"].numpy()
134: 
135:         with torch.no_grad():
136:             if model_type == "segformer":
137:                 outputs = model(pixel_values=image_t)
138:                 logits = outputs.logits
139:                 logits = torch.nn.functional.interpolate(
140:                     logits,
141:                     size=(sample["labels"].shape[0], sample["labels"].shape[1]),
142:                     mode="bilinear",
143:                     align_corners=False,
144:                 )
145:             else:
146:                 logits = model(image_t)
147: 
148:         pred_cls = logits.argmax(dim=1).squeeze(0).cpu().numpy()
149: 
150:         # Denormalize image
151:         img = image_t.squeeze(0).cpu() * std + mean
152:         img = img.permute(1, 2, 0).numpy()
153:         img = np.clip(img, 0, 1)
154: 
155:         # Colorize masks
156:         true_rgb = np.zeros((*mask_true.shape, 3), dtype=np.float32)
157:         pred_rgb = np.zeros((*pred_cls.shape, 3), dtype=np.float32)
158:         for c, color in cmap.items():
159:             true_rgb[mask_true == c] = color
160:             pred_rgb[pred_cls == c] = color
161: 
162:         axes[row, 0].imshow(img)
163:         axes[row, 0].set_title("Original")
164:         axes[row, 0].axis("off")
165:         axes[row, 1].imshow(true_rgb)
166:         axes[row, 1].set_title("Ground Truth")
167:         axes[row, 1].axis("off")
168:         axes[row, 2].imshow(pred_rgb)
169:         axes[row, 2].set_title("Prediction")
170:         axes[row, 2].axis("off")
171: 
172:     legend_patches = [
173:         Patch(color=cmap[c], label=f"{c}: {name}")
174:         for c, name in enumerate(CLASS_NAMES)
175:     ]
176:     fig.legend(
177:         handles=legend_patches,
178:         loc="lower center",
179:         ncol=min(6, NUM_CLASSES),
180:         fontsize=7,
181:     )
182:     plt.tight_layout(rect=[0, 0.05, 1, 1])
183: 
184:     save_path = output_dir / "predictions.png"
185:     plt.savefig(save_path, dpi=150, bbox_inches="tight")
186:     plt.close()
187:     print(f"Visualizations saved: {save_path}")
188: 
189: 
190: # ============================================================================
191: # Model Loading
192: # ============================================================================
193: 
194: 
195: def load_segformer_model(checkpoint_path: Path, device: str):
196:     """Load SegFormer model from checkpoint."""
197:     from transformers import SegformerForSemanticSegmentation
198: 
199:     print(f"Loading SegFormer: {SEGFORMER_MODEL_NAME}")
200:     model = SegformerForSemanticSegmentation.from_pretrained(
201:         SEGFORMER_MODEL_NAME,
202:         num_labels=NUM_CLASSES,
203:         ignore_mismatched_sizes=True,
204:     )
205:     state = torch.load(checkpoint_path, map_location=device, weights_only=True)
206:     model.load_state_dict(state["model_state_dict"])
207:     model.to(device)
208:     model.eval()
209: 
210:     print(f"  Checkpoint epoch: {state.get('epoch', 'unknown')}")
211:     print(f"  Checkpoint mIoU:  {state.get('miou', 'unknown'):.4f}")
212:     return model
213: 
214: 
215: def load_unet_model(checkpoint_path: Path, device: str):
216:     """Load U-Net model from SMP checkpoint."""
217:     import segmentation_models_pytorch as smp
218: 
219:     print(f"Loading U-Net: {UNET_ENCODER} (weights={UNET_ENCODER_WEIGHTS})")
220:     model = smp.Unet(
221:         encoder_name=UNET_ENCODER,
222:         encoder_weights=None,  # Load from checkpoint, not pretrained
223:         in_channels=3,
224:         classes=NUM_CLASSES,
225:     )
226:     state = torch.load(checkpoint_path, map_location=device, weights_only=True)
227:     model.load_state_dict(state["model_state_dict"])
228:     model.to(device)
229:     model.eval()
230: 
231:     print(f"  Checkpoint epoch: {state.get('epoch', 'unknown')}")
232:     print(f"  Checkpoint mIoU:  {state.get('miou', 'unknown'):.4f}")
233:     return model
234: 
235: 
236: # ============================================================================
237: # Main
238: # ============================================================================
239: 
240: 
241: def evaluate(
242:     model_type: str,
243:     checkpoint_path: Path,
244:     output_dir: Path,
245:     device: str = "cpu",
246: ) -> None:
247:     """Run full evaluation and save results."""
248: 
249:     assert model_type in ("segformer", "unet"), \
250:         f"model_type must be 'segformer' or 'unet', got '{model_type}'"
251: 
252:     output_dir = Path(output_dir)
253:     output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
254: 
255:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
256:     # Load model
257:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
258:     if model_type == "segformer":
259:         model = load_segformer_model(checkpoint_path, device)
260:     else:
261:         model = load_unet_model(checkpoint_path, device)
262: 
263:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
264:     # Data
265:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
266:     val_dataset = create_val_dataset(VAL_IMG_DIR, VAL_MASK_DIR)
267:     val_loader = DataLoader(
268:         val_dataset,
269:         batch_size=BATCH_SIZE,
270:         shuffle=False,
271:         num_workers=NUM_WORKERS,
272:         pin_memory=True,
273:     )
274:     print(f"Validation tiles: {len(val_dataset)}")
275: 
276:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
277:     # Inference
278:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
279:     print("\nRunning inference...")
280:     all_preds = []
281:     all_targets = []
282: 
283:     with torch.no_grad():
284:         for batch in tqdm(val_loader, desc="  Evaluating"):
285:             images = batch["pixel_values"].to(device)
286:             masks = batch["labels"]
287: 
288:             if model_type == "segformer":
289:                 outputs = model(pixel_values=images)
290:                 logits = outputs.logits
291:                 logits = torch.nn.functional.interpolate(
292:                     logits,
293:                     size=masks.shape[-2:],
294:                     mode="bilinear",
295:                     align_corners=False,
296:                 )
297:             else:
298:                 logits = model(images)
299: 
300:             all_preds.append(logits.cpu())
301:             all_targets.append(masks)
302: 
303:     all_preds = torch.cat(all_preds, dim=0)
304:     all_targets = torch.cat(all_targets, dim=0)
305: 
306:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
307:     # Metrics
308:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
309:     print("\nComputing metrics...")
310:     metrics = compute_metrics(all_preds, all_targets, NUM_CLASSES)
311: 
312:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
313:     # Results
314:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
315:     print(f"\n{'='*60}")
316:     print(f"EVALUATION RESULTS — {model_type.upper()}")
317:     print(f"{'='*60}")
318:     print(f"  mIoU:           {metrics['miou']:.4f}")
319:     print(f"  mDice:          {metrics['mdice']:.4f}")
320:     print(f"  Pixel Accuracy: {metrics['pixel_accuracy']:.4f}")
321:     print(f"\n  Per-class IoU & Dice:")
322:     print(f"  {'Class':<25s} {'IoU':>8s}  {'Dice':>8s}")
323:     print(f"  {'-'*25} {'-'*8}  {'-'*8}")
324:     for cls_id, name in enumerate(CLASS_NAMES):
325:         iou = metrics["per_class_iou"][cls_id]
326:         dice = metrics["per_class_dice"][cls_id]
327:         print(f"  {name:<25s} {iou:8.4f}  {dice:8.4f}")
328: 
329:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
330:     # Save
331:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
332:     # JSON report
333:     report = {
334:         "model_type": model_type,
335:         "checkpoint": str(checkpoint_path),
336:         "metrics": metrics,
337:     }
338:     report_path = output_dir / "metrics.json"
339:     with open(report_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
340:         json.dump(report, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
341:     print(f"\nMetrics saved: {report_path}")
342: 
343:     # Visualization
344:     print("\nGenerating visualizations...")
345:     generate_visualizations(model, val_dataset, model_type, output_dir, device)
346: 
347:     print(f"\nAll results saved to: {output_dir}")
348: 
349: 
350: # ============================================================================
351: # Entry
352: # ============================================================================
353: 
354: if __name__ == "__main__":
355:     model_type = EVAL_MODEL_TYPE
356:     device = get_device()
357: 
358:     # 自动找 checkpoint 或用手工指定的
359:     if EVAL_CHECKPOINT is not None:
360:         checkpoint_path = Path(EVAL_CHECKPOINT).resolve()
361:     else:
362:         found = auto_find_checkpoint(model_type)
363:         if found is None:
364:             print(f"ERROR: 没有找到 {model_type} 的 checkpoint")
365:             print(f"       请先训练，或在 config.py 设置 EVAL_CHECKPOINT 手工指定路径")
366:             exit(1)
367:         checkpoint_path = found
368:         print(f"自动找到 checkpoint: {checkpoint_path}")
369: 
370:     if not checkpoint_path.exists():
371:         print(f"ERROR: Checkpoint not found: {checkpoint_path}")
372:         exit(1)
373: 
374:     output_dir = f"eval_{checkpoint_path.parent.name}"
375: 
376:     evaluate(
377:         model_type=model_type,
378:         checkpoint_path=checkpoint_path,
379:         output_dir=Path(output_dir),
380:         device=device,
381:     )

(End of file - total 381 lines)
</content>
```
